<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напрямик.html>напрями́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naprjamík</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bluntly, point-blank <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in a blunt manner</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>directly, straight</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:пря.html>пря</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ми́к</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a>, определительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>; неизменяемое.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>на-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-прям-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ик</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<ol><li>bluntly, point-blank <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in a blunt manner</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

***напрячь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напрячь.html>напря́чь</a> (12827)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-прячь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-prjačʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напрячь.html>напря́чь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naprjáčʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напрягать.html>напряга́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flex (a muscle)</li>
<li>to strain (the back, the ears)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stress out</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>пу<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:гать.html>га́ть</a></b>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пускать.html>пуска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">puskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напускать.html>напуска́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napuskátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напустить.html>напусти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to let in, to allow to enter (a large amount of liquid, gas or small items)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to let in (someone)</li>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:напускать.html>напуска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:туман.html>тума́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>napuskátʹ</b> tumánu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to confuse the issue</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to unleash, to sic (an animal) on; to incite (someone) onto <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

<ol><li>to let in, to allow to enter (a large amount of liquid, gas or small items)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to let in (someone)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:напустить.html>напусти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>napustítʹ</b> na sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to feign, to affect (a trait)</span></div></dd>

***напялить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напялить.html>напя́лить</a> (14101)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пялить.html>пя́лить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pjálitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напялить.html>напя́лить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napjálitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напяливать.html>напя́ливать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stretch <i>(on)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vernacular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pull <i>(on)</i>, to get on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стараться.html>стара́ться</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:напялить.html>напя́лить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:слишком.html>сли́шком</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тесный.html>те́сное</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">starátʹsja <b>napjálitʹ</b> na sebjá štó-libo slíškom tésnoje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to squeeze/struggle into smth that is too small for one</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vernacular<span class="ib-comma">,</span> deprecative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to trick out <i>(in)</i>, to dude up <i>(in)</i>, to fig up, to fig out <i>(in)</i></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:раса.html>ра́с</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>па́ш<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ку

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нарастить.html>нарасти́ть</a> (29055)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растить.html>расти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rastítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нарастить.html>нарасти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">narastítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наращивать.html>нара́щивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to grow, to develop, to graft on</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lengthen, to augment</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to intensify, to increase, to build up</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
